            		<h1 class="title" id="page-title">Rioter Talks: PAX South 2015</h1>

With a room of fellow PAX pioneers, they hosted a game design panel and audience Q &amp; A to discuss good and bad champion design. And Urgot.</p>
<p class="rtecenter"><a href="http://www.twitch.tv/pax/c/5961229" target="_blank"><img alt="" src="/sites/default/files/The%20Good%20the%20Bad%20and%20the%20Urgot.png" style="width: 700px; height: 412px;" /></a><br />

    <div class="field field-name-body field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even" property="content:encoded"> <p>Riot Games announced that <em>League of Legends</em> will launch in the fall. Players can <a href="https://signup.leagueoflegends.com/" target="_blank">download and play</a> for free at <a href="https://www.leagueoflegends.com" target="_blank">www.leagueoflegends.com</a>.</p>
